Here is the output of sudo lsof | grep  ubiquity on the installer DVD of Ubuntu 21.04 from Linux Magazine issue 248 July 2021. I had one browser window open looking up something about debconf, and a second tab open about something else I believe. But no other connection. I had also uninstalled anything with PPP in it and a few other things that might be making connections. I don't understand why there seem to be remote files mounted on local folders, and I don't know what fuse.portal is used for. I have never seen that fuse module. But the reason I have not done anything with any of this is not because I am scared or lazy. I have been to several attorneys with what to me and several other people were legitimate and inexplicable issues. What I am finding is that it might be the work of people who have also managed to convince anyone that I contact about it that I am some terrorist trying to trap someone or who knows what. I was turned away from the FBI with a phone in my hand that I tried to tell them was from someone who admitted to hacking it, and it seems like they outhacked the government even. But if so, then it's no wonder all of the government agencies I have been to seeking help were unwilling to help me, and it's no wonder that to this day I still am accused of inaction while at the same time accused of talking about things I am supposed to forget. But that's another story that I would tell elsewhere if I knew someone would listen and not tell me to shut up.
